[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe overflow occurs on a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte heap-allocated region:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Allocated Region:** [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x5020000000d0[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x5020000000d7[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Overflow Address:** [0m[1;36m0x5020000000d7[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after the allocated region[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Allocation Point:** `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` at line [0m[1;36m18[0m[39m in [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fuzz-udev-rule-parse-value.c`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe memory was allocated via `malloc` in the fuzzer harness, and the subsequent [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing in `udev_rule_parse_value` attempted to write one byte beyond the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated buffer boundary.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Shadow Memory Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe ASan shadow memory dump shows:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x502000000080[0m[39m: fa fa [0m[1;36m06[0m[39m fa fa fa [0m[1;36m06[0m[39m fa fa fa[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m07[0m[1;39m][0m[39mfa fa fa [0m[1;36m02[0m[39m fa[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m07[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` indicates a partially addressable region where [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes are valid, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirming that the write occurred exactly at the boundary of the allocated memory.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo obtain a comprehensive understanding of this vulnerability, the following [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents should be examined:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Primary Source File:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The buffer allocation [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m suggests a small input that triggers an edge [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcase[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/udev/fuzz-udev-rule-parse-value.[0m[1;92mc:18[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m22[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m18[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35massert_se[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr = [0m[1;35mmalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39msize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m19[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr, data, size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m20[0m[39m:        str[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msize[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m21[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m22[0m[39m:        r = [0m[1;35mudev_rule_parse_value[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr, &value, &endpos, &is_case_sensitive[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause Identification[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe heap-buffer-overflow occurs in `udev_rule_parse_value` at line [0m[1;36m1223[0m[39m when [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwriting the second null terminator in the escaped + prefix_match code path:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstr[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos + l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Line [0m[1;36m1223[0m[39m - writes beyond allocated buffer[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe function performs in-place string transformation without validating buffer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundaries. Specifically:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **The function assumes extra buffer space**: It writes up to [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m additional bytes [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`*\[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` for prefix_match[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m beyond the processed content[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **The fuzzer allocates minimal space**: Only `size + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` bytes for input of [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`size` bytes[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Production code works by accident**: Rule lines contain multiple key-value [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpairs, providing buffer space after each value[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Critical write locations**:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Non-escaped + prefix_match: writes to `j[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[39m bytes: `*\[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Escaped + prefix_match: writes to `str[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos + l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[39m bytes: `*\[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Both non-prefix cases: write [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m null terminators[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why Previous Patches Would Fail[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is the initial bug report, so no previous patches exist. However, any patch [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat only modifies the fuzzer harness without fixing the underlying function would [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe incorrect, as the function itself lacks bounds checking.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **In-place transformation**: The function modifies the input buffer directly and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturns pointers into it[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Nulstr format**: Results must be terminated by two consecutive null bytes for [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafe interpretation as nulstr[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Prefix handling**: The function supports [0m[32m'e'[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mescaped[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[32m'i'[0m[39m [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mcase-insensitive[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and [0m[32m'p'[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprefix-match[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m flags in any order[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Return values**: `*ret_value` points to processed value, `*ret_endpos` points [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpast closing quote[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Add Bounds Validation to `udev_rule_parse_value`[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe function must validate that writes stay within the input buffer boundaries. [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSince the input is null-terminated, we can use `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to determine the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavailable space.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Calculate input buffer size at function entry**[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter the initial assertions [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m1148[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize_t input_len = [0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Add bounds check before writing in escaped + prefix_match path**[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBefore line [0m[1;36m1220[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwithin the `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mis_prefix_match[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block at line [0m[1;36m1218[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mis_prefix_match[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Check if buffer has space for: content at [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpos-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[32m'*'[0m[39m + two [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpos + l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m >= input_len[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return -EOVERFLOW;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr + pos - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, unescaped, l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    str[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos + l - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'*'[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    str[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos + l[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    str[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos + l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    m = str + pos - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Add bounds check in escaped + non-prefix_match path**[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBefore line [0m[1;36m1227[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39min the `else` block at line [0m[1;36m1226[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Check if buffer has space for: content at m + two [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mm + l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m >= str + input_len[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return -EOVERFLOW;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm, unescaped, l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    m[0m[1;39m[[0m[39ml[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    m[0m[1;39m[[0m[39ml + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Add bounds check in non-escaped + prefix_match path**[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBefore line [0m[1;36m1187[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwithin the `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mis_prefix_match[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mis_prefix_match[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Check if buffer has space for j[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, j[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, j[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m][0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    j[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'*'[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    j[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    j[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Error Code Selection[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mUse `-EOVERFLOW` to indicate buffer space insufficiency, which is semantically [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappropriate for this error condition. This error code already exists in the systemd[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluded via `errno.h`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Supporting Changes[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Include necessary header**: Ensure `<errno.h>` is included in [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/udev/udev-rules.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlikely already present, but verify[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Fix Is Optimal[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Addresses root cause**: Adds bounds checking to the function itself, not just [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe fuzzer[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves existing behavior**: Only rejects inputs that would cause buffer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow; all valid inputs work as before[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Minimal API change**: No function signature modification required[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Performance impact**: Negligible - one `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call at function entry and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msimple comparisons before writes[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Consistency**: Follows the codebase pattern of validating buffer operations [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39msee `strxcpyx.c` examples[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Security**: Prevents potential exploitation through crafted udev rules[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The in-place transformation logic remains unchanged[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All pointer arithmetic and buffer manipulations are preserved[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The nulstr format [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtwo consecutive nulls[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is maintained[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Return values and semantics stay the same[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only inputs that would overflow are rejected with an error[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Addressing the Evaluation Report[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix directly addresses line [0m[1;36m1223[0m[39m where the overflow occurs:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Before: `str[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos + l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;` executes unconditionally[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- After: Only executes if `pos + l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m < input_len`, otherwise returns `-EOVERFLOW`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis prevents the [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write beyond the [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte allocated region described in the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreport.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Testing Considerations[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix should not break existing tests because:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. All test cases in `test-udev-rules.c` use `[0m[1;35mstrdup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which allocates sufficient[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspace[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Production usage via `[0m[1;35mrule_add_line[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` operates on complete rule lines with [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mample buffer space[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The fuzzer will need a testcase that exercises the new error path, but this is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpected behavior for malformed/insufficient input[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Minimal risk**: The only side effect is that inputs which previously caused [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mundefined behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer overflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now return an error code. This is the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdesired behavior and improves robustness. No valid use cases should be affected [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msince:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Production rule files provide adequate buffer space[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Test cases allocate proper buffers[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Any caller that doesn't provide adequate buffer space has a bug that should be [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcaught[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
